  676. It is almost ridiculous how much we love this diffuser. Having received it as a thank you gift from some houseguests back in December, we've used it every night since. And sometimes multiple times throughout the day too. Because of this gift, we are now regular haunts at the local healthy store's essential oil aisle.<br /><br />The Zaq Allay is a small Aromatherapy Diffuser. This means that it takes water and essential oil and transforms it into a mist with the touch of a button. The unit comes with a base, an unpluggable cord, an inner clear plastic cone, and the outer (in our case blue) plastic cone. To operate, you unplug the cord from the unit, take off the plastic cones, and fill the reservoir with water to the inner rim. Then you drop in a few drops of your choice of oils, replace the cones on top, and plug the unit back into the cord. The first press of the button turns the unit on and mist immediately begins flowing, a light also lights up the power button and the colored cone at the top. A second press of the button turns off the light on the cone, but the power button light still remains on. A third press turns the unit off.<br /><br />I like that you can see the mist coming out of the machine. It is fascinating to watch (at least the cats think so) and the fact that it happens immediately is pretty magical too. If left turn on it will run for several hours (3-4) although once it ran the entire night and was still going when we woke up the next morning (there was still water in the reservoir, it wasn't running dry). Once the reservoir empties, it automatically shuts itself off. So you can set it and forget about it or use it as a sleep aid without worrying. I usually put about 5 drops into the machine and I can smell it pretty strongly on my entire 2nd floor (2 bedrooms, a hall and a bath) and sometimes I can even smell it downstairs in my living room when it's been running upstairs so I feel like it does a great job scenting the air and providing moisture.<br /><br />Cleanup is easy. I just use a damp cloth on the inside of the reservoir and I haven't noticed any buildup of oil. The only time I've ever had problems with the unit is when I overfilled the reservoir and it took awhile to get to a manageable level for the diffuser to operate correctly, but that was my fault, not the diffusers. With the correct amount of water it has worked perfectly every time.<br /><br />I really do love this thing and am now considering a bigger one from the same company for my downstairs. They're fun to place with, make the place smell great, and are neat to watch.<br /><br />Review by M. Reynard 2015viding moisture.<br /><br />Cleanup is easy.   757. I really like this diffuser and it makes my whole downstairs smell awesome. It's definitely a nice alternative to scented candles.<br /><br />But here's a few notes on maintenance:<br /><br />Build-up around the metallic ring will lessen the diffuser's efficacy and shorten it's diffusing duration, to the point where the diffuser is unusable (only turns on for a few seconds and then turns off). This is easily solved, however, by cleaning it with rubbing alcohol. Instead of filling it up with water, I filled it up with rubbing alcohol and let it sit for about an hour. Afterwards, I dumped out the alcohol and scrubbed out the inside with some q-tips and paper towels to clean the metal ring. After that, it worked like new!<br /><br />Also, as of recently, instead of tap water, I've been using distilled water that I got from the grocery store. I'm finding that the build-up from hard water as well as the oil interacting with the hard water is pretty much no longer an issue.

UPDATED from 2 stars to 4 stars! ***Update*** I think that when I wrote the review below, I must have gotten diffusers from a production run that was sub-par, because my later ZAQ Allay diffusers have run for many months trouble-free, the disks do not need changing as often (4-6 months between disks!), and the diffuser runs for much longer (2-3 hours instead of 30-60 minutes). I'm very pleased that these have worked so well in the long run. They are definitely my preferred diffuser, especially for the price! I have also had one repaired under warranty. Bombay Electronics was very fast and courteous in honoring the 1-year warranty that these come with. ************** V V V *Original Review Below* V V V Short review: - This diffuser is quite nice, when it works. - Very easy to use. - These do eventually fail (1yr or less by my experience). - ZAQ has *NO* customer service at all. - Plan to pay a couple extra bucks every few months for a new disc to keep it running. - Plan to buy a new one when the discs are no longer are the problem. Full story: I bought one of these and loved it. It does exactly what it advertised and I wanted -- quietly diffuses essential oils into the air, refreshing my house and those in it. I like the slight gurgly sound from the water when it runs (you can hear it in a quiet room, but I don't find it to be intrusively loud). It works for one mid-sized room. Runs about 30-45 minutes for me (dry environment). Pretty, quiet, hassle-free. I used it often for three months and really liked it, so I ordered a second one for another room. Then the first one stopped working. I had rinsed it regularly as recommended to prevent buildup. But it had the problem covered in a lot of reviews where the unit still turns on but doesn't mist/diffuse and shuts off prematurely. Nothing could make it revive. But hey, I already had a second unit, so I just used that. The second one worked just as well, but it had a brown grime in the bottom by about the seconduse, so it got rinsed after most uses to prevent any buildup. I contacted ZAQ through their website about both problems, but never got a response. I saw their video about replacing the ceramic disc, but since you can't order it through the website and there was no link to purchase it elsewhere, I didn't pursue it further at the time. Sadly, 2 months after I got the second unit, it too met its demise in the same manner as the first. I'd read the reviews about this problem before purchasing these, so I was disappointed but not surprised. Clearly it's a consistent problem with this product if both of mine failed in the same way at about the same usage point, and it's happening to a lot of other users. Therefore, I went back to ZAQ's website, which has a link to contact them, along with a video about this common problem. I contacted them again through the website, and also mailed a paper copy since there is no option for phone contact. I waited a week, then emailed them again. I have never gotten any response to any contact attempt, in spite of including my contact information on each message. Since there is no way through their website to buy the part, no link to an external seller, and no product name to search for, I searched around and found the part here on Amazon. http://smile.amazon.com/dp/B00JK0UVUU The only good news here is that the repair part immediately got my diffuser working just like new! Bad news is that the part came with no instructions, and even though I'd watched the how-to video, it took two tries to get the disc installed correctly. I'm waiting for the second disc to arrive to see if it repairs the second diffuser that's currently a paperweight. Update: The second replacement disc got the second diffuser working just fine right away, and it DOES have instructions on the back of the package, along with an aftermarket UPC label, so I think the first one just had the directions covered up. I'm disappointed that there is no customer service, or better information for customers. I'm disappointed that the diffuser only works to a point. I'm disappointed that ZAQ knows this is a problem, but doesn't include a spare disk with their products or make any effort to resolve the problem for the consumer. I'm disappointed that I have to pay for a repair part in such a short time. I'm pleased that the diffuser is working again, that it looks nice, and that it does what it says it should -- when it's working. In short, assuming I have to replace the disc on each unit every two months, that's $5-6 a month to run them after the purchase price. I'm ok with that price point, and I'm ok with how the diffuser works when it's working. If you're not, this might not be the droi.... diffuser you're looking for. Move along. Update July 2015: I downrated this from 3 stars to 2 stars this time, and here's why: 2 months after replacing the discs, one of the diffusers quit working, permanently. The motor made a dreadful sound and it never ran again. It had been cared for well, so it seems the motor goes bad. The other diffuser worked for 6 more months (and needed two replacement discs during that time) and then that motor died as well. Assuming you pay $30 for this, that's $75 a year for new diffusers and discs. Seems you might as well buy an expensive one! Considering that I cleaned these regularly and they did nothing more than sit on a shelf and run, I'm disappointed in the quality of this product. But I'm more disappointed in the utter failure of ZAQ to properly address these issues in this product and their failure to provide any customer service. I wouldn't recommend it. Update Nov 2015: I added stars to this! It seems whatever issues they had with the diffusers have been better addressed. The dead unit in which the motor failed was repaired under warranty by Bombay Electronics. I now own three of these. They work great and I love them!
